***буйвол.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:буйвол.html>бу́йвол</a> (20862)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*byvolъ</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bujьvolъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буйвол.html>бу́йвол</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bújvol</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буйвол.html>бу́йвола</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буйвол.html>бу́йволы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буйвол.html>бу́йволов</a></b>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bujьnъ</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:буйство.html>бу́йство</a> (20933)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бу́й(ный)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">búj(nyj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буйство.html>бу́йство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bújstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буйство.html>бу́йства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буйство.html>бу́йства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буйство.html>бу́йств</a></b>)

<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table class="morfotable ru" style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse; max-width:300px;" cellpadding="3" rules="all">

<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Illustration_Fagus_sylvatica0_clean.jpg/220px-Illustration_Fagus_sylvatica0_clean.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="355" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Illustration_Fagus_sylvatica0_clean.jpg/330px-Illustration_Fagus_sylvatica0_clean.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Illustration_Fagus_sylvatica0_clean.jpg/440px-Illustration_Fagus_sylvatica0_clean.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1427" data-file-height="2304" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:бук.html>бук</a></div></div></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*buky</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*bōkijā</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beech</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бук.html>бук</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">buk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бук.html>бу́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бук.html>бу́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бук.html>бу́ков</a></b>)
</p>

***буква.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:буква.html>бу́ква</a> (1659)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">бꙋкꙑ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">buky</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*buky</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буква.html>бу́ква</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">búkva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буква.html>бу́квы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буква.html>бу́квы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буква.html>бу́кв</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>letter <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a symbol in an alphabet</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:буква.html>бу́ква</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>búkva</b> zakóna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the letter of the law</span></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:буквальный.html>буква́льный</a> (12853)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буква.html>бу́ква</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">búkva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-альный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-alʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">littéral</i>. ***буксир.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:буксир.html>букси́р</a> (13403)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1705. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">boegseren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">puxar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pulsāre</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буксир.html>букси́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">buksír</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буксир.html>букси́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буксир.html>букси́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буксир.html>букси́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tug, tugboat, towboat</li>
<li>tow, towrope, towline
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуть.html>тяну́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:буксир.html>букси́ре</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tjanútʹ na <b>buksíre</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tow</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:буксир.html>букси́р</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vzjatʹ na <b>buksír</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take in tow; to give a helping hand (figuratively)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***буксовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:буксовать.html>буксова́ть</a> (20848)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бу́кса</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">búksa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">metal box in which a train axle rotates and into which oil is poured</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буксовать.html>буксова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">buksovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">забуксова́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to skid, to spin around without traction <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a car or its wheels</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stall, to be in a gridlock
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2018</b>,  <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9A%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BA" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ru:Кровосток">Кровосток</a></span> (lyrics and music),  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вишенка.html>Ви́шенка</a></span>”, in  <cite><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ЧБ</span></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">что́-то <a href = vnd.unilang:должный.html>должно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помогать.html>помога́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:буксовать.html>буксу́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ирония.html>иро́ния</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> «что́-то» <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вколотить.html>вколоти́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> «что́-то» <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> штаке́т</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Štó-to dolžnó pomogátʹ, kogdá <b>buksújet</b> irónija<br />Nádo najtí éto “štó-to” i vkolotítʹ éto “štó-to” v štakét</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Something must abet, when irony <b>has a stun</b><br />One must find “suttin” and slot this “suttin” in the bun</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***бульон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бульон.html>бульо́н</a> (11344)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bouillon</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бульон.html>бульо́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bulʹón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бульон.html>бульо́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бульон.html>бульо́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бульон.html>бульо́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>broth, bouillon <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">water in which food (meat or vegetable etc) has been boiled</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>clear soup</li></ol>

***бумага.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́га</a> (550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Uncertain. Believed to be from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Persian" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Persian">Middle Persian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pal">pmbk'</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cotton</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> through some Mediterranean term for cotton wool and/or cloth, since first attestations of the root in the 15th and 16th centuries are mostly with a now obsolete sense, the only remnant of which in modern active vocabulary is <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопчатобумажный.html>хлопчатобума́жный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xlopčatobumažnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">made from cotton</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First paper was imported to Russia from Italy and Greece.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́га</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bumága</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́ги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́г</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́га</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bumága</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бумажник.html>бума́жник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bumážnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бумажник.html>бума́жника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бумажник.html>бума́жники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бумажник.html>бума́жников</a></b>)

<ol><li>wallet</li>
<li>papermaker, worker in the paper industry</li></ol>
